 maine bharat ke liye 16 saal pehle apana pehla test khelaa tha or aaj mujhe lagata he ki aage badhane kaa samay aa gaya he
 i was like a boy in India who dreams of playing for his country
 maine kabhi nahin sochaa tha ki meri yatra itani lambii or itani paripurna rahegi
 '' dravid ke saath bisisiai adhyaksh en shrinivasana or purv bhartiya captain anil kumble bhi maujuud the
 He said, "no dream can be fulfilled alone
 main un logon kaa shukriya adaa karnaa chaahunga, jinhone mujhe cricket sikhaaya or mujh par bharosa rakhaa
 My junior coaches and various junior national camps in Bengaluru made me so obsessed with cricket
 " Dravid said, "my coaches have improved my cricket at the international level and that has helped to enhance my personality
 physio or trainron ne mujhe feet banane ke liye kaaphi mehnat kii, jo aasaan kaam nahin he, jisaki badaulat main 30 kii umr ke antim padaav main bhi kheltaa rahaa
 "he never gets any credit to the selectors in India, but he trusted me many times, i didn't trust myself so much and i am thankful to him for that," he said
 main jitne bhi captainon kii aguwai main khelaa, unhone meraa netritv kiya or mujhe prerit kiya
 Most of all i would like to thank the teams i played with
 â€™â€™ Dravid said he had many wonderful memories associated with his teammates, including some of the greatest players in the game
 unhone kaha, â€˜â€˜main kariyar ke shuru ke dinon main karnataka kii team se khelaa or ve saal mere liye kaaphi manoranjak or sikh hasil karne vaale rahe
 "I was fortunate to be part of the glorious era in the Indian team, in which India played some of the best cricket at home and abroad
" team ke kai saathi mahaan ban gaye, bharat main hi nahin, balki puri cricket duniya main
 i admire him a lot, i have learned a lot from him and i am saying goodbye to cricket with great memories of his time spent with him and strong friendship
 yah shandaar bhent he
 '' dravid ne kaha ki unhone hameshaa cricket kii khel bhaavana ko barkaraar rakhane kii koshish kii he
 "my attitude to cricket has always been simple - give everything to the team, play with respect and always keep the spirit of the game," he said
 mujhe ummid he ki maine isamen se kuch chijen kii hai
 i failed many times, but i did not stop trying
 isliye main thode dukh ke saath ise chhod rahaa hum, lekin saath hi mujhe garv bhi he
 '' unhone apane lambey kariyar ke dauraan mili samarthan ke liye cricket prashansakon kaa shukriya adaa kiya
 Dravid said, "I would also like to thank Indian cricket fans here and around the world
" cricket bhaagyashaalee he ki aap log iske prashansak hai or main isliye bhaagyashaalee hum ki main aapke saamne khel paaya
 It is an honor to represent India and to represent myself and i have always taken this thing seriously
 â€™â€™ The tour of Australia was a disappointment, with 24 of them
 25 ke ausat se aath pariyon main keval 194 ran banaae
 Even more frustrating was that Dravid, known for his strong technique, was bowled six out of eight times
 australian daure ke baad dravid ke bhavishya par atakalein lagaai ja rahi thim or ab unke sanyas lene ke faisle se nigahen ek anya mahaan ballebaaj vivies lakshmana par lag gai hai, jinke liye bhi yah daura niraashajanak rahaa
 Dravid retired from ODI cricket in England last year and was selected in the ODI squad after making a surprise decision given his brilliant performance (three centuries) during the Test series against England
 'da walâ€™ ke naam se mashhoor dravid ne june, 1996 main aagaaj kiya tha, haalanki vah indian premier lig ke paanchaven charan main jaipur kii frenchiji rajasthan royles kii aguwai karenge
 The comments dravid ne 164 test maichon main 13,288 ran banaae hai or vah tendulkar (188 test main 15,470 ran) ke baad sarvaadhik ran banane vaale duusare cricketer hai
 He 52
 31 ke ausat se 36 shatak or 63 ardhashatak jade hai
 His best score was 270 runs for Pakistan
 unhone april 1996 se sitambar 2011 tak vanade cricket khelaa or 344 vanade main 12 shatak, 83 ardhashatak ke saath 39
 He scored 10,889 runs at an average of 16
 dravid ke naam test maichon main sarvaadhik 210 kaich lapakane kaa vishwa record bhi he
 He beat Mark Waugh in slip catches
 iske atirikt unke vanade main 196 kaich hai
 Asked how long he took to decide on retirement, Dravid said, "for the last one year i have been assessing after every series
 jab main australia se aayaa, to isamen bhaawanaaon ko dur rakhana chahta tha
 i spoke to Sachin and teammates and everyone was supportive of it

 yah kaaphi chizon par vichaar ke baad kiya gaya
 These decisions are based on many things
 â€™â€™ The 39-year-old Dravid became the first player to retire in three aging Indian cricket players â€” Sachin Tendulkar and VVS Laxman â€” after a disappointing Test tour to Australia

 i played my first Test for India 16 years ago and today i feel that the time has come to move forward

 " dravid ne kaha, â€˜â€˜antarrashtriya str par mere kochon ne meri cricket main sudhaar kiya or jisase mere vyaktitv ko nikharane main madad mili

 â€™â€™ unhone kaha, â€˜â€˜bharat main chayankartaaon ko kabhi bhi koi shrey nahin miltaa, lekin unhone kai baar mujh par bharosa jataayaa, balki itnaa bharosa mujhe khud par nahin tha or main iske liye unka shukraguzaar hum
 All the captains i played led, led and inspired me
 sabase zyada main un tiimon kaa shukriya adaa karnaa chaahunga, jinke saath main khelaa
 '' dravid ne kaha ki unki team ke saathiyon ke saath kai shandaar yaaden judi hai, jisamen khel ke kuch mahaan khilaadi bhi shaamil hai
 He said, "I played with the Karnataka team in the early days of my career and those years were very entertaining and learning for me
 â€™â€™ unhone kaha, â€˜â€˜bhartiya team main main us shandaar yug kaa hissaa hokar bhaagyashaalee rahaa, jisamen bharat ne gharelu or videshi sarajameen par kuch behtareen cricket khelaa
 Many teammates became great, not only in India, but in the entire cricket world
 main unki kaaphi prashansa karata hum, maine unase kaaphi kuch siikhaa he or main cricket ko unke saath bitaye gaye samay kii shandaar yaadon or majboot dosti ke saath alavida kah rahaa hum
 This is a great gift
 â€™â€™ Dravid said that he has always tried to maintain the sporting spirit of cricket
 unhone kaha, â€˜â€˜cricket ke liye meraa ravaiya hameshaa saral rahaa he - team ke liye sarvasv do, sammaan se khelo or khel bhaavana ko hameshaa barkaraar rakho

 main kai baar asafal rahaa, lekin maine koshish karnaa nahin choda

 â€™â€™ He thanked cricket fans for the support he received during his long career
 dravid ne kaha, â€˜â€˜main yahaan or duniya bhar ke bhartiya cricket prashansakon kaa bhi shukriya karnaa chaahunga

 bharat kaa pratinidhitiv karnaa or khud kaa pratinidhitiv karnaa sammaan kii baat he or is cheez ko maine hameshaa hi gambhirtha se liya he
 '' australia kaa daura kaaphi niraashajanak rahaa, jisamen unhone 24
 Only 194 runs in eight innings at an average of 25
 isse bhi hatashapurna rahaa ki apni majboot takanic ke liye mashhoor dravid aath main se chah baar bold hue
 There was speculation about Dravid's future after the Australian tour and now his decision to retire has turned his eyes on another legendary batsman, VVS Laxman, for whom the tour was also disappointing
 dravid ne pichley saal england main vanade cricket se sanyas le liya tha or england ke khilaaf test shrunkhlaa ke dauraan unke shandaar pradarshan (teen shatak) ko dekhte hue unhen hairaani bharaa faisla karte hue vanade team main chunaa gaya tha
 Dravid, known as 'the Wall', made his debut in June 1996, though he would lead Jaipur franchise Rajasthan Royals in the fifth leg of the Indian Premier League
 tippaniyan Dravid has scored 13,288 runs in 164 Tests and is the second highest cricketer after Tendulkar (15,470 runs in 188 Tests)
 unhone 52
 Has scored 36 centuries and 63 half-centuries at an average of 31
 pakistan ke liye 270 ran unka sarvshereshth score rahaa
 He played ODI cricket from April 1996 to September 2011 and scored 34 centuries in 344 odis, 39 with 83 fifties
 16 ke ausat se 10,889 ran banaae
 Dravid also holds the world record for catching the most 210 catches in Test matches
 unhone slip kaichon main mark wa ko pahada tha

 '' central board of secondary ajukeshan (CBSE) ne haal hi main nae rules tay kiye hai
 Teachers will no longer engage students in buses and engage in non-academic work
 sibiesai ne beete shuukravaar ko desh ke tamaam privet skulon ko yah sunishchit karne ko kaha he ki shikshancanteen kii vyavasthadekhane samet bason main bacchon ke saath travel karne vaale gamecadamik kaary na karen
 The new order has been taken by CBSE following complaints from teachers
 aise kaaryon main sanlipt hone ke baad shikshakon ke paas bacchon ko padhaane laayak urja nahin bachati
 In view of this, there were also disclosures in the complaints that private schools are getting teachers multitasking
 ve unhen fees jamaa karne kii prakriya samet clerk ke kaam main bhi laga leti hai
 Due to the cost saving process, teachers are not able to do their main work
 shiksha kaa adhikaar kya kahata he
 
 
 Chapter 4 of the Right to Education Act states that no teacher can be placed anywhere except during the ten-year census, any natural calamity and duty during elections
 iske baavjood shikshakon ko skool bason main bacchon ko laane-pahunchane ke liye bhi niyukt bhi kiya gaya he
 Now in this regard, CBSE has asked the school principal to ensure that they take care of the progress made in this direction and this should not happen from now on

 loksabhaa chunaav 2019 kaa aupchaarik elaan ho gaya he
 This time elections will be held in the country in seven phases
 haalanki desh ke 22 rajyon main ek charan main matdaan honge
 While Uttar Pradesh, Bihar and West Bengal will have elections in seven phases
 vahiin, jammu-kashmir main kul chah loksabhaa siton ke liye paanch charan main vot daale jaaenge
 Chief Election Commissioner Sunil Arora announced a seven-phase polling, announcing the dates for the Lok Sabha elections
 desh ke 22 rajyon main ek hi charan main vot daale jaaenge
 These include Andhra Pradesh, Arunachal, Goa, Gujarat, Haryana, Kerala, Meghalaya, Mizoram, Nagaland, Punjab, Sikkim, Tamil Nadu, Telangana, Uttarakhand, Andaman Nicobar, Dadanagar Haveli, Daman Dweep, Lakshadweep, Delhi, Punducherry and Chandigarh
 In one phase, votes will be cast on the Lok Sabha seats
 desh ke teen rajya hai jahaan saaton charnon main vot daale jaaenge
 These include Lok Sabha seats in the states of Bihar, Uttar Pradesh and West Bengal
 in teenon rajyon main kul 162 loksabhaa siten aati hai

 unhone 2014 ke upachunaav main congress pratyaashee ashok raav patil ko haraakar is seat par jeet hasil kii thi

 seat kaa siyaasi itihaashvahin seat ke itihaas kii baat karen to pichley teen chunaavon se yani 2009 se yah seat bijepi ke khate main hai
 In the 2009 Lok Sabha elections, bjp's Gopinath Munde received 5,53,994 votes, defeating Ramesh Baburao of NCP
 2014 main gopinath munde duusari baar phir bijepi ke tikat se chunaav lade or jeet hasil kii
 In 2014, Gopinath Munde died in a road accident, 9 days after he was sworn in as a Union Minister in the Modi government
 iske baad bid loksabhaa seat par upachunaav hue or gopinath munde kii beti preetam munde ne chunaav maidan main utrin
 Pritam Munde defeated his rival and Congress leader Ashok Shankarrao by securing 9,22,416 votes
 iske alaava bid loksabhaa seat ke antargat 6 vidhansabha siten aati hai
